Dashboard API API documentation version v2

http://localhost:8081/v2/instance/{instanceName}

Object Rocket Control Panel Stats 2.0 Dashboard API

The Object Rocket Control Panel Stats 2.0 Dashboard API allows the Object Rocket Control Panel GUI to generate dashboards and graphs from the stats of redis and mongodb instances. Currently mongodb available statistics are derived from MongoDB Server Status Output.

Dashboard root

Create, edit or delete instance stats graphs to a dashboard.

/dashboard/{dbname}

The dbname parameter will determine whether the dashboard graphs represent instance level or db level statistics having the db name present. By default the dashboard will show instance level stats so this value will be "instance".

/dashboard/{dbname}/{dashboardId} post get delete

Save, retrieve or delete dashboards

post

save dashboard

get

retrieve dashboard

delete

delete dashboard

post /dashboard/{dbname}/{dashboardId}

save dashboard

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • dbname: required (string)
  • dashboardId: required (string)

Headers

  • X-Auth-Account: (string)

    Example:

    54f0fe50d151602b3f27d72a
  • X-Auth-Token: (string)

    Example:

    IjBlNzAwNWZkYjA0NjQyZjQ4MDI3NWRmYjUxYTJkMThlIg.B9KSNQ.MZQE29dx46h7Mbb15KjLLroZ9dw

Body

Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded

Form Parameters
  • name: required (string)

    Dashboard Name

    Example:

    My Dashboard

HTTP status code 200

Headers

  • Access-Control-Allow-Origin: (string)

    Example:

    *

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

{"message": "Dashboard saved"}

get /dashboard/{dbname}/{dashboardId}

retrieve dashboard

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • dbname: required (string)
  • dashboardId: required (string)

Headers

  • X-Auth-Account: (string)

    Example:

    54f0fe50d151602b3f27d72a
  • X-Auth-Token: (string)

    Example:

    IjBlNzAwNWZkYjA0NjQyZjQ4MDI3NWRmYjUxYTJkMThlIg.B9KSNQ.MZQE29dx46h7Mbb15KjLLroZ9dw

HTTP status code 200

Headers

  • Access-Control-Allow-Origin: (string)

    Example:

    *

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema#",
  "id": "http://jsonschema.net",
  "type": "object",
  "title": "Dashboard schema.",
  "description": "Schema for Dashboard data.",
  "name": "/",
  "properties": {
    "graphs": {
      "id": "http://jsonschema.net/graphs",
      "type": "array",
      "title": "Graphs schema.",
      "name": "graphs",
      "items": {
        "id": "http://jsonschema.net/graphs/0",
        "type": "object",
        "title": "0 schema.",
        "name": "0",
        "properties": {
          "_id": {
            "id": "http://jsonschema.net/graphs/0/_id",
            "type": "integer",
            "title": "_id schema.",
            "description": "id of graph saved to dashboard.",
            "name": "_id",
            "default": 4,
            "enum": [
              null,
              4
            ]
          }
        },
        "required": [
          "_id"
        ]
      },
      "required": [
        "0"
      ]
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "graphs"
  ]
}

Example:

{
  "graphs": [
    {
      "_id": 1,
      "_id": 2,
      "_id": 3,
      "_id": 4
    }
  ]
}

HTTP status code 404

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

{"message": "Dashboard not found"}

delete /dashboard/{dbname}/{dashboardId}

delete dashboard

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • dbname: required (string)
  • dashboardId: required (string)

Headers

  • X-Auth-Account: (string)

    Example:

    54f0fe50d151602b3f27d72a
  • X-Auth-Token: (string)

    Example:

    IjBlNzAwNWZkYjA0NjQyZjQ4MDI3NWRmYjUxYTJkMThlIg.B9KSNQ.MZQE29dx46h7Mbb15KjLLroZ9dw

HTTP status code 200

OK

Headers

  • Access-Control-Allow-Origin: (string)

    Example:

    *

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

{"message": "Dashboard deleted"}

/dashboard/{dbname}/{dashboardId}/{graphId} post put delete

Choosing a date range (1 hour, 1 day, 1 week) and an available stat, a customer can create a graph showing data from all of the primaries of an instance and then save it to a dashboard.

post

create / add graph to / for stats dashboard

put

update graph for stats dashboard

delete

remove graph from dashboard

post /dashboard/{dbname}/{dashboardId}/{graphId}

create / add graph to / for stats dashboard

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • dbname: required (string)
  • dashboardId: required (string)
  • graphId: required (string)

Headers

  • X-Auth-Account: (string)

    Example:

    54f0fe50d151602b3f27d72a
  • X-Auth-Token: (string)

    Example:

    IjBlNzAwNWZkYjA0NjQyZjQ4MDI3NWRmYjUxYTJkMThlIg.B9KSNQ.MZQE29dx46h7Mbb15KjLLroZ9dw

Body

Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded

Form Parameters
  • time_range: required (string)

    Time range of statistics

    Example:

    1 day
  • stat_type: required (string)

    Type of statistic

    Example:

    current connections

HTTP status code 200

Headers

  • Access-Control-Allow-Origin: (string)

    Example:

    *

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema#",

put /dashboard/{dbname}/{dashboardId}/{graphId}

update graph for stats dashboard

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • dbname: required (string)
  • dashboardId: required (string)
  • graphId: required (string)

Headers

  • X-Auth-Account: (string)

    Example:

    54f0fe50d151602b3f27d72a
  • X-Auth-Token: (string)

    Example:

    IjBlNzAwNWZkYjA0NjQyZjQ4MDI3NWRmYjUxYTJkMThlIg.B9KSNQ.MZQE29dx46h7Mbb15KjLLroZ9dw

Body

Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded

Form Parameters
  • time_range: (string)

    Time range of statistics

    Example:

    1 day
  • stat_type: (string)

    Type of statistic

    Example:

    current connections

HTTP status code 200

Headers

  • Access-Control-Allow-Origin: (string)

    Example:

    *

Body

Type: application/json

    "points": {
      "show": false
    }
  }
]

delete /dashboard/{dbname}/{dashboardId}/{graphId}

remove graph from dashboard

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • dbname: required (string)
  • dashboardId: required (string)
  • graphId: required (string)

Headers

  • X-Auth-Account: (string)

    Example:

    54f0fe50d151602b3f27d72a
  • X-Auth-Token: (string)

    Example:

OK

Headers

/dashboard/{dbname}/stats get

By default four graphs will be created on the dashboard with either one of these instance level stats: connections.current, globalLock.activeClients.readers, globalLock.activeClients.total, globalLock.activeClients.writers, globalLock.currentQueue.readers, globalLock.currentQueue.total, globalLock.currentQueue.writers, mem.mapped, mem.resident, mem.virtual, opcounters.command, opcounters.delete, opcounters.getmore, opcounters.insert, opcounters.query, opcounters.update

get

get available stat names for instance or db
